text: "154\n5\n2\n9: b\n22\nE\n1. My faith looks up to thee, Thou Lamb of Cal-va-ry; Sa- vior di-vine! Now hear me\n#\nHo\n77\n9:22\n5-6-2\nMY FAITH LOOKS UP TO THEE. 6s & 4s.\n\342\227\217\ngf\nwhile I pray; Take all my guilt away; 0, let me from this day Be whol-ly thine.\nH\n386.\nChrist, our Confidence.\n1 MY faith looks up to thee,\nThou Lamb of Calvary;\nSavior divine!\nNow hear me while I pray;\nTake all my guilt away;\nOh let me from this day\nBe wholly thine.\n2 May thy rich grace impart\nStrength to my fainting heart,\nMy zeal inspire;\nAs thou hast died for me,\nOh! may my love to thee,\nPure, warm, and changeless be,\nA living fire.\n3 While life\'s dark maze I tread,\nAnd griefs around me spread,\nBe thou my guide;\nBid darkness turn to day,\nWipe sorrow\'s tears away,\nNor let me ever stray\nFrom thee aside.\n4 When ends life\'s transient dream,\nWhen death\'s cold sullen stream\nShall o\'er me roll;\nBlest Savior, then in love,\nFear and distrust remove:\nOh! bear me. safe above-\nA ransomed soul.\nSpiritual Songs.\n66\n-0\n387.\nWorthy the Lamb.\n1 \"GLORY to God on high !\"\nLet heaven and earth reply,\nPraise ye\nhis name !\"\342\201\271\nHis love and grace adore,\nWho all our sorrows bore;\nSing aloud evermore-\n\"Worthy the Lamb.\"\n2 Ye who surround the throne,\nCheerfully join in one,\nPraising his name:\n66\nHis love and grace adore,\nWho all our sorrows bore;\nSing aloud evermore\n\'Worthy the Lamb.\"\n3 Join all ye ransomed race\nOur Lord and God to bless;\nPraise ye his name:\nOn him we fix our choice,\nIn him we will rejoice,\nShouting with heart and voice-\n\"Worthy the Lamb.\"\n4 Soon must we close our race,\nYet will we never cease\nPraising his name:\nBut as we upward wing,\nHail him our gracious King,\nAnd through the heavens sing-\n\"Worthy the Lamb.\"\nell"
